I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Default values for function props prevents reactivity when passed to child components
### Describe the bug

If you have some component that takes a function as a prop and passes that on to child components, when the component provides a default value for that prop, changing the value of the prop will trigger reactivity with that component but will not trigger reactivity within any child components. This does not occur if the prop is a string type, for example, or if a default is not specified. This behaviour is the case regardless of whether the default value is ever used.

This manifested as fairly subtle failure in our usecase and took some time to isolate.

### Reproduction

https://svelte.dev/playground/1bdd3298b7574da5bffe6a21ef8b6086?version=5.36.13

    10	## What is Svelte?
    11	
    12	Svelte is a new way to build web applications. It's a compiler that takes your declarative components and converts them into efficient JavaScript that surgically updates the DOM.
    13	
    14	Learn more at the [Svelte website](https://svelte.dev), or stop by the [Discord chatroom](https://svelte.dev/chat).
    15	
    16	## Supporting Svelte

    21	
    22	Funds donated via Open Collective will be used for compensating expenses related to Svelte's development such as hosting costs. If sufficient donations are received, funds may also be used to support Svelte's development more directly.

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/3-transform/client/visitors/shared/component.js:
     1	/** @import { BlockStatement, Expression, ExpressionStatement, Identifier, MemberExpression, Pattern, Property, SequenceExpression, Statement } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../../types.js' */
     4	import { dev, is_ignored } from '../../../../../state.js';
     5	import { get_attribute_chunks, object } from '../../../../../utils/ast.js';
     6	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     7	import { add_svelte_meta, build_bind_this, Memoizer, validate_binding } from '../shared/utils.js';
     8	import { build_attribute_value } from '../shared/element.js';
     9	import { build_event_handler } from './events.js';
    10	import { determine_slot } from '../../../../../utils/slot.js';
    11	
    12	/**
    13	 * @param {AST.Component | AST.SvelteComponent | AST.SvelteSelf} node
    14	 * @param {string} component_name
    15	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    16	 * @returns {Statement}
    17	 */
    18	export function build_component(node, component_name, context) {
    19	        /**
    20	         * @type {Expression}
    21	         */
    22	        const anchor = context.state.node;
    23	        /** @type {Array<Property[] | Expression>} */
    24	        const props_and_spreads = [];
    25	        /** @type {Array<() => void>} */
    26	        const delayed_props = [];
    27	
    28	        /** @type {ExpressionStatement[]} */
    29	        const lets = [];
    30	
    31	        /** @type {Record<string, typeof context.state>} */
    32	        const states = {
    33	                default: {
    34	                        ...context.state,
    35	                        scope: node.metadata.scopes.default,
    36	                        transform: { ...context.state.transform }
    37	                }
    38	        };
    39	
    40	        /** @type {Record<string, AST.TemplateNode[]>} */
    41	        const children = {};
    42	
    43	        /** @type {Record<string, Expression[]>} */
    44	        const events = {};
    45	
    46	        const memoizer = new Memoizer();
    47	
    48	        /** @type {Property[]} */
    49	        const custom_css_props = [];
    50	
    51	        /** @type {Identifier | MemberExpression | SequenceExpression | null} */
    52	        let bind_this = null;
    53	
    54	        /** @type {ExpressionStatement[]} */
    55	        const binding_initializers = [];
    56	
    57	        const is_component_dynamic =
    58	                node.type === 'SvelteComponent' || (node.type === 'Component' && node.metadata.dynamic);
    59	
    60	        // The variable name used for the component inside $.component()
    61	        const intermediate_name =
    62	                node.type === 'Component' && node.metadata.dynamic
    63	                        ? context.state.scope.generate(node.name)
    64	                        : '$$component';
    65	
    66	        /**
    67	         * If this component has a slot property, it is a named slot within another component. In this case
    68	         * the slot scope applies to the component itself, too, and not just its children.
    69	         */
    70	        let slot_scope_applies_to_itself = !!determine_slot(node);
    71	
    72	        /**
    73	         * Components may have a children prop and also have child nodes. In this case, we assume
    74	         * that the child component isn't using render tags yet and pass the slot as $$slots.default.
    75	         * We're not doing it for spread attributes, as this would result in too many false positives.
    76	         */
    77	        let has_children_prop = false;
    78	
    79	        /**
    80	         * @param {Property} prop
    81	         * @param {boolean} [delay]
    82	         */
    83	        function push_prop(prop, delay = false) {
    84	                const do_push = () => {
    85	                        const current = props_and_spreads.at(-1);
    86	                        const current_is_props = Array.isArray(current);
    87	                        const props = current_is_props ? current : [];
    88	                        props.push(prop);
    89	                        if (!current_is_props) {
    90	                                props_and_spreads.push(props);
    91	                        }
    92	                };
    93	
    94	                if (delay) {
    95	                        delayed_props.push(do_push);
    96	                } else {
    97	                        do_push();
    98	                }
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        if (slot_scope_applies_to_itself) {
   102	                for (const attribute of node.attributes) {
   103	                        if (attribute.type === 'LetDirective') {
   104	                                lets.push(/** @type {ExpressionStatement} */ (context.visit(attribute)));
   105	                        }
   106	                }
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        for (const attribute of node.attributes) {
   110	                if (attribute.type === 'LetDirective') {
   111	                        if (!slot_scope_applies_to_itself) {
   112	                                lets.push(/** @type {ExpressionStatement} */ (context.visit(attribute, states.default)));
   113	                        }
   114	                } else if (attribute.type === 'OnDirective') {
   115	                        if (!attribute.expression) {
   116	                                context.state.analysis.needs_props = true;
   117	                        }
   118	
   119	                        let handler = build_event_handler(
   120	                                attribute.expression,
   121	                                attribute.metadata.expression,
   122	                                context
   123	                        );
   124	
   125	                        if (attribute.modifiers.includes('once')) {
   126	                                handler = b.call('$.once', handler);
   127	                        }
   128	
   129	                        (events[attribute.name] ||= []).push(handler);
   130	                } else if (attribute.type === 'SpreadAttribute') {
   131	                        const expression = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(attribute));
   132	
   133	                        if (attribute.metadata.expression.has_state) {
   134	                                props_and_spreads.push(
   135	                                        b.thunk(
   136	                                                attribute.metadata.expression.has_await || attribute.metadata.expression.has_call
   137	                                                        ? b.call('$.get', memoizer.add(expression, attribute.metadata.expression.has_await))
   138	                                                        : expression
   139	                                        )
   140	                                );
   141	                        } else {
   142	                                props_and_spreads.push(expression);
   143	                        }
   144	                } else if (attribute.type === 'Attribute') {
   145	                        if (attribute.name.startsWith('--')) {
   146	                                custom_css_props.push(
   147	                                        b.init(
   148	                                                attribute.name,
   149	                                                build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context, (value, metadata) => {
   150	                                                        // TODO put the derived in the local block
   151	                                                        return metadata.has_call || metadata.has_await
   152	                                                                ? b.call('$.get', memoizer.add(value, metadata.has_await))
   153	                                                                : value;
   154	                                                }).value
   155	                                        )
   156	                                );
   157	                                continue;
   158	                        }
   159	
   160	                        if (attribute.name === 'slot') {
   161	                                slot_scope_applies_to_itself = true;
   162	                        }
   163	
   164	                        if (attribute.name === 'children') {
   165	                                has_children_prop = true;
   166	                        }
   167	
   168	                        const { value, has_state } = build_attribute_value(
   169	                                attribute.value,
   170	                                context,
   171	                                (value, metadata) => {
   172	                                        if (!metadata.has_state && !metadata.has_await) return value;
   173	
   174	                                        // When we have a non-simple computation, anything other than an Identifier or Member expression,
   175	                                        // then there's a good chance it needs to be memoized to avoid over-firing when read within the
   176	                                        // child component (e.g. `active={i === index}`)
   177	                                        const should_wrap_in_derived =
   178	                                                metadata.has_await ||
   179	                                                get_attribute_chunks(attribute.value).some((n) => {
   180	                                                        return (
   181	                                                                n.type === 'ExpressionTag' &&
   182	                                                                n.expression.type !== 'Identifier' &&
   183	                                                                n.expression.type !== 'MemberExpression'
   184	                                                        );
   185	                                                });
   186	
   187	                                        return should_wrap_in_derived
   188	                                                ? b.call('$.get', memoizer.add(value, metadata.has_await))
   189	                                                : value;
   190	                                }
   191	                        );
   192	
   193	                        if (has_state) {
   194	                                push_prop(b.get(attribute.name, [b.return(value)]));
   195	                        } else {
   196	                                push_prop(b.init(attribute.name, value));
   197	                        }
   198	                } else if (attribute.type === 'BindDirective') {
   199	                        const expression = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(attribute.expression));
   200	
   201	                        if (
   202	                                dev &&
   203	                                attribute.name !== 'this' &&
   204	                                !is_ignored(node, 'ownership_invalid_binding') &&
   205	                                // bind:x={() => x.y, y => x.y = y} will be handled by the assignment expression binding validation
   206	                                attribute.expression.type !== 'SequenceExpression'
   207	                        ) {
   208	                                const left = object(attribute.expression);
   209	                                const binding = left && context.state.scope.get(left.name);
   210	
   211	                                if (binding?.kind === 'bindable_prop' || binding?.kind === 'prop') {
   212	                                        context.state.analysis.needs_mutation_validation = true;
   213	                                        binding_initializers.push(
   214	                                                b.stmt(
   215	                                                        b.call(
   216	                                                                '$$ownership_validator.binding',
   217	                                                                b.literal(binding.node.name),
   218	                                                                b.id(is_component_dynamic ? intermediate_name : component_name),
   219	                                                                b.thunk(expression)
   220	                                                        )
   221	                                                )
   222	                                        );
   223	                                }
   224	                        }
   225	
   226	                        if (expression.type === 'SequenceExpression') {
   227	                                if (attribute.name === 'this') {
   228	                                        bind_this = attribute.expression;
   229	                                } else {
   230	                                        const [get, set] = expression.expressions;
   231	                                        const get_id = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('bind_get'));
   232	                                        const set_id = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('bind_set'));
   233	
   234	                                        context.state.init.push(b.var(get_id, get));
   235	                                        context.state.init.push(b.var(set_id, set));
   236	
   237	                                        push_prop(b.get(attribute.name, [b.return(b.call(get_id))]));
   238	                                        push_prop(b.set(attribute.name, [b.stmt(b.call(set_id, b.id('$$value')))]));
   239	                                }
   240	                        } else {
   241	                                if (
   242	                                        dev &&
   243	                                        expression.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
   244	                                        context.state.analysis.runes &&
   245	                                        !is_ignored(node, 'binding_property_non_reactive')
   246	                                ) {
   247	                                        validate_binding(context.state, attribute, expression);
   248	                                }
   249	
   250	                                if (attribute.name === 'this') {
   251	                                        bind_this = attribute.expression;
   252	                                } else {
   253	                                        const is_store_sub =
   254	                                                attribute.expression.type === 'Identifier' &&
   255	                                                context.state.scope.get(attribute.expression.name)?.kind === 'store_sub';
   256	
   257	                                        // Delay prop pushes so bindings come at the end, to avoid spreads overwriting them
   258	                                        if (is_store_sub) {
   259	                                                push_prop(
   260	                                                        b.get(attribute.name, [b.stmt(b.call('$.mark_store_binding')), b.return(expression)]),
   261	                                                        true
   262	                                                );
   263	                                        } else {
   264	                                                push_prop(b.get(attribute.name, [b.return(expression)]), true);
   265	                                        }
   266	
   267	                                        const assignment = b.assignment(
   268	                                                '=',
   269	                                                /** @type {Pattern} */ (attribute.expression),
   270	                                                b.id('$$value')
   271	                                        );
   272	
   273	                                        push_prop(
   274	                                                b.set(attribute.name, [b.stmt(/** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(assignment)))]),
   275	                                                true
   276	                                        );
   277	                                }
   278	                        }
   279	                } else if (attribute.type === 'AttachTag') {
   280	                        const evaluated = context.state.scope.evaluate(attribute.expression);
   281	
   282	                        let expression = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(attribute.expression));
   283	
   284	                        if (attribute.metadata.expression.has_state) {
   285	                                expression = b.arrow(
   286	                                        [b.id('$$node')],
   287	                                        b.call(
   288	                                                evaluated.is_function ? expression : b.logical('||', expression, b.id('$.noop')),
   289	                                                b.id('$$node')
   290	                                        )
   291	                                );
   292	                        }
   293	
   294	                        push_prop(b.prop('init', b.call('$.attachment'), expression, true));
   295	                }
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        delayed_props.forEach((fn) => fn());
   299	
   300	        if (slot_scope_applies_to_itself) {
   301	                context.state.init.push(...lets);
   302	        }
   303	
   304	        if (Object.keys(events).length > 0) {
   305	                const events_expression = b.object(
   306	                        Object.keys(events).map((name) =>
   307	                                b.init(name, events[name].length > 1 ? b.array(events[name]) : events[name][0])
   308	                        )
   309	                );
   310	                push_prop(b.init('$$events', events_expression));
   311	        }
   312	
   313	        /** @type {Statement[]} */
   314	        const snippet_declarations = [];
   315	
   316	        /** @type {import('estree').Property[]} */
   317	        const serialized_slots = [];
   318	
   319	        // Group children by slot
   320	        for (const child of node.fragment.nodes) {
   321	                if (child.type === 'SnippetBlock') {
   322	                        // the SnippetBlock visitor adds a declaration to `init`, but if it's directly
   323	                        // inside a component then we want to hoist them into a block so that they
   324	                        // can be used as props without creating conflicts
   325	                        context.visit(child, {
   326	                                ...context.state,
   327	                                init: snippet_declarations
   328	                        });
   329	
   330	                        push_prop(b.prop('init', child.expression, child.expression));
   331	
   332	                        // Interop: allows people to pass snippets when component still uses slots
   333	                        serialized_slots.push(
   334	                                b.init(child.expression.name === 'children' ? 'default' : child.expression.name, b.true)
   335	                        );
   336	
   337	                        continue;
   338	                }
   339	
   340	                let slot_name = determine_slot(child) ?? 'default';
   341	
   342	                (children[slot_name] ||= []).push(child);
   343	        }
   344	
   345	        // Serialize each slot
   346	        for (const slot_name of Object.keys(children)) {
   347	                const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (
   348	                        context.visit(
   349	                                {
   350	                                        ...node.fragment,
   351	                                        // @ts-expect-error
   352	                                        nodes: children[slot_name]
   353	                                },
   354	                                slot_name === 'default'
   355	                                        ? slot_scope_applies_to_itself
   356	                                                ? context.state
   357	                                                : states.default
   358	                                        : {
   359	                                                        ...context.state,
   360	                                                        scope: node.metadata.scopes[slot_name],
   361	                                                        transform: { ...context.state.transform }
   362	                                                }
   363	                        )
   364	                );
   365	
   366	                if (block.body.length === 0) continue;
   367	
   368	                const slot_fn = b.arrow(
   369	                        [b.id('$$anchor'), b.id('$$slotProps')],
   370	                        b.block([
   371	                                ...(slot_name === 'default' && !slot_scope_applies_to_itself ? lets : []),
   372	                                ...block.body
   373	                        ])
   374	                );
   375	
   376	                if (slot_name === 'default' && !has_children_prop) {
   377	                        if (
   378	                                lets.length === 0 &&
   379	                                children.default.every(
   380	                                        (node) =>
   381	                                                node.type !== 'SvelteFragment' ||
   382	                                                !node.attributes.some((attr) => attr.type === 'LetDirective')
   383	                                )
   384	                        ) {
   385	                                // create `children` prop...
   386	                                push_prop(
   387	                                        b.init(
   388	                                                'children',
   389	                                                dev ? b.call('$.wrap_snippet', b.id(context.state.analysis.name), slot_fn) : slot_fn
   390	                                        )
   391	                                );
   392	
   393	                                // and `$$slots.default: true` so that `<slot>` on the child works
   394	                                serialized_slots.push(b.init(slot_name, b.true));
   395	                        } else {
   396	                                // create `$$slots.default`...
   397	                                serialized_slots.push(b.init(slot_name, slot_fn));
   398	
   399	                                // and a `children` prop that errors
   400	                                push_prop(b.init('children', b.id('$.invalid_default_snippet')));
   401	                        }
   402	                } else {
   403	                        serialized_slots.push(b.init(slot_name, slot_fn));
   404	                }
   405	        }
   406	
   407	        if (serialized_slots.length > 0) {
   408	                push_prop(b.init('$$slots', b.object(serialized_slots)));
   409	        }
   410	
   411	        if (
   412	                !context.state.analysis.runes &&
   413	                node.attributes.some((attribute) => attribute.type === 'BindDirective')
   414	        ) {
   415	                push_prop(b.init('$$legacy', b.true));
   416	        }
   417	
   418	        const props_expression =
   419	                props_and_spreads.length === 0 ||
   420	                (props_and_spreads.length === 1 && Array.isArray(props_and_spreads[0]))
   421	                        ? b.object(/** @type {Property[]} */ (props_and_spreads[0]) || [])
   422	                        : b.call(
   423	                                        '$.spread_props',
   424	                                        ...props_and_spreads.map((p) => (Array.isArray(p) ? b.object(p) : p))
   425	                                );
   426	
   427	        /** @param {Expression} node_id */
   428	        let fn = (node_id) => {
   429	                return b.call(
   430	                        // TODO We can remove this ternary once we remove legacy mode, since in runes mode dynamic components
   431	                        // will be handled separately through the `$.component` function, and then the component name will
   432	                        // always be referenced through just the identifier here.
   433	                        is_component_dynamic
   434	                                ? intermediate_name
   435	                                : /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(b.member_id(component_name))),
   436	                        node_id,
   437	                        props_expression
   438	                );
   439	        };
   440	
   441	        if (bind_this !== null) {
   442	                const prev = fn;
   443	
   444	                fn = (node_id) => {
   445	                        return build_bind_this(bind_this, prev(node_id), context);
   446	                };
   447	        }
   448	
   449	        const statements = [...snippet_declarations, ...memoizer.deriveds(context.state.analysis.runes)];
   450	
   451	        if (is_component_dynamic) {
   452	                const prev = fn;
   453	
   454	                fn = (node_id) => {
   455	                        return b.call(
   456	                                '$.component',
   457	                                node_id,
   458	                                b.thunk(
   459	                                        /** @type {Expression} */ (
   460	                                                context.visit(node.type === 'Component' ? b.member_id(component_name) : node.expression)
   461	                                        )
   462	                                ),
   463	                                b.arrow(
   464	                                        [b.id('$$anchor'), b.id(intermediate_name)],
   465	                                        b.block([...binding_initializers, b.stmt(prev(b.id('$$anchor')))])
   466	                                )
   467	                        );
   468	                };
   469	        } else {
   470	                statements.push(...binding_initializers);
   471	        }
   472	
   473	        if (Object.keys(custom_css_props).length > 0) {
   474	                if (context.state.metadata.namespace === 'svg') {
   475	                        // this boils down to <g><!></g>
   476	                        context.state.template.push_element('g', node.start);
   477	                } else {
   478	                        // this boils down to <svelte-css-wrapper style='display: contents'><!></svelte-css-wrapper>
   479	                        context.state.template.push_element('svelte-css-wrapper', node.start);
   480	                        context.state.template.set_prop('style', 'display: contents');
   481	                }
   482	
   483	                context.state.template.push_comment();
   484	                context.state.template.pop_element();
   485	
   486	                statements.push(
   487	                        b.stmt(b.call('$.css_props', anchor, b.thunk(b.object(custom_css_props)))),
   488	                        b.stmt(fn(b.member(anchor, 'lastChild'))),
   489	                        b.stmt(b.call('$.reset', anchor))
   490	                );
   491	        } else {
   492	                context.state.template.push_comment();
   493	
   494	                statements.push(add_svelte_meta(fn(anchor), node, 'component', { componentTag: node.name }));
   495	        }
   496	
   497	        memoizer.apply();
   498	
   499	        const async_values = memoizer.async_values();
   500	
   501	        if (async_values) {
   502	                return b.stmt(
   503	                        b.call(
   504	                                '$.async',
   505	                                anchor,
   506	                                async_values,
   507	                                b.arrow([b.id('$$anchor'), ...memoizer.async_ids()], b.block(statements))
   508	                        )
   509	                );
   510	        }
   511	
   512	        return statements.length > 1 ? b.block(statements) : statements[0];
   513	}
   514

    26	/**
    27	 * @param {((value?: number) => number)} fn
    28	 * @param {1 | -1} [d]
    29	 * @returns {number}
    30	 */
    31	export function update_prop(fn, d = 1) {
    32	        const value = fn();
    33	        fn(value + d);
    34	        return value;
    35	}
    36

    38	 * @param {((value?: number) => number)} fn

    43	        const value = fn() + d;
    44	        fn(value);
    45	        return value;

    48	/**
    49	 * The proxy handler for rest props (i.e. `const { x, ...rest } = $props()`).
    50	 * Is passed the full `$$props` object and excludes the named props.
    51	 * @type {ProxyHandler<{ props: Record<string | symbol, unknown>, exclude: Array<string | symbol>, name?: string }>}}
    52	 */
    53	const rest_props_handler = {
    54	        get(target, key) {
    55	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return;
    56	                return target.props[key];
    57	        },
    58	        set(target, key) {
    59	                if (DEV) {
    60	                        // TODO should this happen in prod too?
    61	                        e.props_rest_readonly(`${target.name}.${String(key)}`);
    62	                }
    63	
    64	                return false;
    65	        },
    66	        getOwnPropertyDescriptor(target, key) {
    67	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return;
    68	                if (key in target.props) {
    69	                        return {
    70	                                enumerable: true,
    71	                                configurable: true,
    72	                                value: target.props[key]
    73	                        };
    74	                }
    75	        },
    76	        has(target, key) {
    77	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return false;
    78	                return key in target.props;
    79	        },
    80	        ownKeys(target) {
    81	                return Reflect.ownKeys(target.props).filter((key) => !target.exclude.includes(key));
    82	        }
    83	};
    84	
    85	/**
    86	 * @param {Record<string, unknown>} props
    87	 * @param {string[]} exclude
    88	 * @param {string} [name]
    89	 * @returns {Record<string, unknown>}
    90	 */
    91	/*#__NO_SIDE_EFFECTS__*/
    92	export function rest_props(props, exclude, name) {
    93	        return new Proxy(
    94	                DEV ? { props, exclude, name, other: {}, to_proxy: [] } : { props, exclude },
    95	                rest_props_handler
    96	        );
    97	}

    99	/**
   100	 * The proxy handler for legacy $$restProps and $$props
   101	 * @type {ProxyHandler<{ props: Record<string | symbol, unknown>, exclude: Array<string | symbol>, special: Record<string | symbol, (v?: unknown) => unknown>, version: Source<number>, parent_effect: Effect }>}}
   102	 */
   103	const legacy_rest_props_handler = {
   104	        get(target, key) {
   105	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return;
   106	                get(target.version);
   107	                return key in target.special ? target.special[key]() : target.props[key];
   108	        },
   109	        set(target, key, value) {
   110	                if (!(key in target.special)) {
   111	                        var previous_effect = active_effect;
   112	
   113	                        try {
   114	                                set_active_effect(target.parent_effect);
   115	
   116	                                // Handle props that can temporarily get out of sync with the parent
   117	                                /** @type {Record<string, (v?: unknown) => unknown>} */
   118	                                target.special[key] = prop(
   119	                                        {
   120	                                                get [key]() {
   121	                                                        return target.props[key];
   122	                                                }
   123	                                        },
   124	                                        /** @type {string} */ (key),
   125	                                        PROPS_IS_UPDATED
   126	                                );
   127	                        } finally {
   128	                                set_active_effect(previous_effect);
   129	                        }
   130	                }
   131	
   132	                target.special[key](value);
   133	                update(target.version); // $$props is coarse-grained: when $$props.x is updated, usages of $$props.y etc are also rerun
   134	                return true;
   135	        },
   136	        getOwnPropertyDescriptor(target, key) {
   137	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return;
   138	                if (key in target.props) {
   139	                        return {
   140	                                enumerable: true,
   141	                                configurable: true,
   142	                                value: target.props[key]
   143	                        };
   144	                }
   145	        },
   146	        deleteProperty(target, key) {
   147	                // Svelte 4 allowed for deletions on $$restProps
   148	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return true;
   149	                target.exclude.push(key);
   150	                update(target.version);
   151	                return true;
   152	        },
   153	        has(target, key) {
   154	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return false;
   155	                return key in target.props;
   156	        },
   157	        ownKeys(target) {
   158	                return Reflect.ownKeys(target.props).filter((key) => !target.exclude.includes(key));
   159	        }
   160	};

   162	/**
   163	 * @param {Record<string, unknown>} props
   164	 * @param {string[]} exclude
   165	 * @returns {Record<string, unknown>}
   166	 */
   167	export function legacy_rest_props(props, exclude) {
   168	        return new Proxy(
   169	                {
   170	                        props,
   171	                        exclude,
   172	                        special: {},
   173	                        version: source(0),
   174	                        // TODO this is only necessary because we need to track component
   175	                        // destruction inside `prop`, because of `bind:this`, but it
   176	                        // seems likely that we can simplify `bind:this` instead
   177	                        parent_effect: /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect)
   178	                },
   179	                legacy_rest_props_handler
   180	        );
   181	}
   182	
   183	/**
   184	 * The proxy handler for spread props. Handles the incoming array of props
   185	 * that looks like `() => { dynamic: props }, { static: prop }, ..` and wraps
   186	 * them so that the whole thing is passed to the component as the `$$props` argument.
   187	 * @template {Record<string | symbol, unknown>} T
   188	 * @type {ProxyHandler<{ props: Array<T | (() => T)> }>}}
   189	 */
   190	const spread_props_handler = {
   191	        get(target, key) {
   192	                let i = target.props.length;
   193	                while (i--) {
   194	                        let p = target.props[i];
   195	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   196	                        if (typeof p === 'object' && p !== null && key in p) return p[key];
   197	                }
   198	        },
   199	        set(target, key, value) {
   200	                let i = target.props.length;
   201	                while (i--) {
   202	                        let p = target.props[i];
   203	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   204	                        const desc = get_descriptor(p, key);
   205	                        if (desc && desc.set) {
   206	                                desc.set(value);
   207	                                return true;
   208	                        }
   209	                }
   210	                return false;
   211	        },
   212	        getOwnPropertyDescriptor(target, key) {
   213	                let i = target.props.length;
   214	                while (i--) {
   215	                        let p = target.props[i];
   216	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   217	                        if (typeof p === 'object' && p !== null && key in p) {
   218	                                const descriptor = get_descriptor(p, key);
   219	                                if (descriptor && !descriptor.configurable) {
   220	                                        // Prevent a "Non-configurability Report Error": The target is an array, it does
   221	                                        // not actually contain this property. If it is now described as non-configurable,
   222	                                        // the proxy throws a validation error. Setting it to true avoids that.
   223	                                        descriptor.configurable = true;
   224	                                }
   225	                                return descriptor;
   226	                        }
   227	                }
   228	        },
   229	        has(target, key) {
   230	                // To prevent a false positive `is_entry_props` in the `prop` function
   231	                if (key === STATE_SYMBOL || key === LEGACY_PROPS) return false;
   232	
   233	                for (let p of target.props) {
   234	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   235	                        if (p != null && key in p) return true;
   236	                }
   237	
   238	                return false;
   239	        },
   240	        ownKeys(target) {
   241	                /** @type {Array<string | symbol>} */
   242	                const keys = [];
   243	
   244	                for (let p of target.props) {
   245	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   246	                        if (!p) continue;
   247	
   248	                        for (const key in p) {
   249	                                if (!keys.includes(key)) keys.push(key);
   250	                        }
   251	
   252	                        for (const key of Object.getOwnPropertySymbols(p)) {
   253	                                if (!keys.includes(key)) keys.push(key);
   254	                        }
   255	                }
   256	
   257	                return keys;
   258	        }
   259	};
   260	
   261	/**
   262	 * @param {Array<Record<string, unknown> | (() => Record<string, unknown>)>} props
   263	 * @returns {any}
   264	 */
   265	export function spread_props(...props) {
   266	        return new Proxy({ props }, spread_props_handler);
   267	}
   268	
   269	/**
   270	 * This function is responsible for synchronizing a possibly bound prop with the inner component state.
   271	 * It is used whenever the compiler sees that the component writes to the prop, or when it has a default prop_value.
   272	 * @template V
   273	 * @param {Record<string, unknown>} props
   274	 * @param {string} key
   275	 * @param {number} flags
   276	 * @param {V | (() => V)} [fallback]
   277	 * @returns {(() => V | ((arg: V) => V) | ((arg: V, mutation: boolean) => V))}
   278	 */
   279	export function prop(props, key, flags, fallback) {
   280	        var runes = !legacy_mode_flag || (flags & PROPS_IS_RUNES) !== 0;
   281	        var bindable = (flags & PROPS_IS_BINDABLE) !== 0;
   282	        var lazy = (flags & PROPS_IS_LAZY_INITIAL) !== 0;
   283	
   284	        var fallback_value = /** @type {V} */ (fallback);
   285	        var fallback_dirty = true;
   286	
   287	        var get_fallback = () => {
   288	                if (fallback_dirty) {
   289	                        fallback_dirty = false;
   290	
   291	                        fallback_value = lazy
   292	                                ? untrack(/** @type {() => V} */ (fallback))
   293	                                : /** @type {V} */ (fallback);
   294	                }
   295	
   296	                return fallback_value;
   297	        };
   298	
   299	        /** @type {((v: V) => void) | undefined} */
   300	        var setter;
   301	
   302	        if (bindable) {
   303	                // Can be the case when someone does `mount(Component, props)` with `let props = $state({...})`
   304	                // or `createClassComponent(Component, props)`
   305	                var is_entry_props = STATE_SYMBOL in props || LEGACY_PROPS in props;
   306	
   307	                setter =
   308	                        get_descriptor(props, key)?.set ??
   309	                        (is_entry_props && key in props ? (v) => (props[key] = v) : undefined);
   310	        }
   311	
   312	        var initial_value;
   313	        var is_store_sub = false;
   314	
   315	        if (bindable) {
   316	                [initial_value, is_store_sub] = capture_store_binding(() => /** @type {V} */ (props[key]));
   317	        } else {
   318	                initial_value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
   319	        }
   320	
   321	        if (initial_value === undefined && fallback !== undefined) {
   322	                initial_value = get_fallback();
   323	
   324	                if (setter) {
   325	                        if (runes) e.props_invalid_value(key);
   326	                        setter(initial_value);
   327	                }
   328	        }
   329	
   330	        /** @type {() => V} */
   331	        var getter;
   332	
   333	        if (runes) {
   334	                getter = () => {
   335	                        var value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
   336	                        if (value === undefined) return get_fallback();
   337	                        fallback_dirty = true;
   338	                        return value;
   339	                };
   340	        } else {
   341	                getter = () => {
   342	                        var value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
   343	
   344	                        if (value !== undefined) {
   345	                                // in legacy mode, we don't revert to the fallback value
   346	                                // if the prop goes from defined to undefined. The easiest
   347	                                // way to model this is to make the fallback undefined
   348	                                // as soon as the prop has a value
   349	                                fallback_value = /** @type {V} */ (undefined);
   350	                        }
   351	
   352	                        return value === undefined ? fallback_value : value;
   353	                };
   354	        }
   355	
   356	        // prop is never written to — we only need a getter
   357	        if (runes && (flags & PROPS_IS_UPDATED) === 0) {
   358	                return getter;
   359	        }
   360	
   361	        // prop is written to, but the parent component had `bind:foo` which
   362	        // means we can just call `$$props.foo = value` directly
   363	        if (setter) {
   364	                var legacy_parent = props.$$legacy;
   365	
   366	                return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
   367	                        if (arguments.length > 0) {
   368	                                // We don't want to notify if the value was mutated and the parent is in runes mode.
   369	                                // In that case the state proxy (if it exists) should take care of the notification.
   370	                                // If the parent is not in runes mode, we need to notify on mutation, too, that the prop
   371	                                // has changed because the parent will not be able to detect the change otherwise.
   372	                                if (!runes || !mutation || legacy_parent || is_store_sub) {
   373	                                        /** @type {Function} */ (setter)(mutation ? getter() : value);
   374	                                }
   375	
   376	                                return value;
   377	                        }
   378	
   379	                        return getter();
   380	                };
   381	        }
   382	
   383	        // Either prop is written to, but there's no binding, which means we
   384	        // create a derived that we can write to locally.
   385	        // Or we are in legacy mode where we always create a derived to replicate that
   386	        // Svelte 4 did not trigger updates when a primitive value was updated to the same value.
   387	        var overridden = false;
   388	
   389	        var d = ((flags & PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE) !== 0 ? derived : derived_safe_equal)(() => {
   390	                overridden = false;
   391	                return getter();
   392	        });
   393	
   394	        if (DEV) {
   395	                d.label = key;
   396	        }
   397	
   398	        // Capture the initial value if it's bindable
   399	        if (bindable) get(d);
   400	
   401	        var parent_effect = /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect);
   402	
   403	        return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
   404	                if (arguments.length > 0) {
   405	                        const new_value = mutation ? get(d) : runes && bindable ? proxy(value) : value;
   406	
   407	                        set(d, new_value);
   408	                        overridden = true;
   409	
   410	                        if (fallback_value !== undefined) {
   411	                                fallback_value = new_value;
   412	                        }
   413	
   414	                        return value;
   415	                }
   416	
   417	                // special case — avoid recalculating the derived if we're in a
   418	                // teardown function and the prop was overridden locally, or the
   419	                // component was already destroyed (this latter part is necessary
   420	                // because `bind:this` can read props after the component has
   421	                // been destroyed. TODO simplify `bind:this`
   422	                if ((is_destroying_effect && overridden) || (parent_effect.f & DESTROYED) !== 0) {
   423	                        return d.v;
   424	                }
   425	
   426	                return get(d);
   427	        };
   428	}
   429

    20	 * @param {Binding} binding

    24	export function is_state_source(binding, analysis) {
    25	        return (
    26	                (binding.kind === 'state' || binding.kind === 'raw_state') &&
    27	                (!analysis.immutable || binding.reassigned || analysis.accessors)
    28	        );
    29	}

    31	/**
    32	 * @param {Identifier} node
    33	 * @param {ClientTransformState} state
    34	 * @returns {Expression}
    35	 */
    36	export function build_getter(node, state) {
    37	        if (Object.hasOwn(state.transform, node.name)) {
    38	                const binding = state.scope.get(node.name);
    39	
    40	                // don't transform the declaration itself
    41	                if (node !== binding?.node) {
    42	                        return state.transform[node.name].read(node);
    43	                }
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        return node;
    47	}

    49	/**
    50	 * @param {FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression | ArrowFunctionExpression} node
    51	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    52	 * @returns {Pattern[]}
    53	 */
    54	function get_hoisted_params(node, context) {
    55	        const scope = context.state.scope;
    56	
    57	        /** @type {Identifier[]} */
    58	        const params = [];
    59	
    60	        /**
    61	         * We only want to push if it's not already present to avoid name clashing
    62	         * @param {Identifier} id
    63	         */
    64	        function push_unique(id) {
    65	                if (!params.find((param) => param.name === id.name)) {
    66	                        params.push(id);
    67	                }
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
    71	                let binding = scope.get(reference);
    72	
    73	                if (binding !== null && !scope.declarations.has(reference) && binding.initial !== node) {
    74	                        if (binding.kind === 'store_sub') {
    75	                                // We need both the subscription for getting the value and the store for updating
    76	                                push_unique(b.id(binding.node.name));
    77	                                binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (scope.get(binding.node.name.slice(1)));
    78	                        }
    79	
    80	                        let expression = context.state.transform[reference]?.read(b.id(binding.node.name));
    81	
    82	                        if (
    83	                                // If it's a destructured derived binding, then we can extract the derived signal reference and use that.
    84	                                // TODO this code is bad, we need to kill it
    85	                                expression != null &&
    86	                                typeof expression !== 'function' &&
    87	                                expression.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    88	                                expression.object.type === 'CallExpression' &&
    89	                                expression.object.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    90	                                expression.object.callee.name === '$.get' &&
    91	                                expression.object.arguments[0].type === 'Identifier'
    92	                        ) {
    93	                                push_unique(b.id(expression.object.arguments[0].name));
    94	                        } else if (
    95	                                // If we are referencing a simple $$props value, then we need to reference the object property instead
    96	                                (binding.kind === 'prop' || binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') &&
    97	                                !is_prop_source(binding, context.state)
    98	                        ) {
    99	                                push_unique(b.id('$$props'));
   100	                        } else if (
   101	                                // imports don't need to be hoisted
   102	                                binding.declaration_kind !== 'import'
   103	                        ) {
   104	                                // create a copy to remove start/end tags which would mess up source maps
   105	                                push_unique(b.id(binding.node.name));
   106	                                // rest props are often accessed through the $$props object for optimization reasons,
   107	                                // but we can't know if the delegated event handler will use it, so we need to add both as params
   108	                                if (binding.kind === 'rest_prop' && context.state.analysis.runes) {
   109	                                        push_unique(b.id('$$props'));
   110	                                }
   111	                        }
   112	                }
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        if (dev) {
   116	                // this is a little hacky, but necessary for ownership validation
   117	                // to work inside hoisted event handlers
   118	
   119	                /**
   120	                 * @param {AssignmentExpression | UpdateExpression} node
   121	                 * @param {{ next: () => void, stop: () => void }} context
   122	                 */
   123	                function visit(node, { next, stop }) {
   124	                        if (validate_mutation(node, /** @type {any} */ (context), node) !== node) {
   125	                                params.push(b.id('$$ownership_validator'));
   126	                                stop();
   127	                        } else {
   128	                                next();
   129	                        }
   130	                }
   131	
   132	                walk(/** @type {Node} */ (node), null, {
   133	                        AssignmentExpression: visit,
   134	                        UpdateExpression: visit
   135	                });
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        return params;
   139	}
   140	
   141	/**
   142	 * @param {FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression | ArrowFunctionExpression} node
   143	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   144	 * @returns {Pattern[]}
   145	 */
   146	export function build_hoisted_params(node, context) {
   147	        const hoisted_params = get_hoisted_params(node, context);
   148	        node.metadata.hoisted_params = hoisted_params;
   149	
   150	        /** @type {Pattern[]} */
   151	        const params = [];
   152	
   153	        if (node.params.length === 0) {
   154	                if (hoisted_params.length > 0) {
   155	                        // For the event object
   156	                        params.push(b.id(context.state.scope.generate('_')));
   157	                }
   158	        } else {
   159	                for (const param of node.params) {
   160	                        params.push(/** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(param)));
   161	                }
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        params.push(...hoisted_params);
   165	        return params;
   166	}
   167	
   168	/**
   169	 * @param {Binding} binding
   170	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   171	 * @param {string} name
   172	 * @param {Expression | null} [initial]
   173	 * @returns
   174	 */
   175	export function get_prop_source(binding, state, name, initial) {
   176	        /** @type {Expression[]} */
   177	        const args = [b.id('$$props'), b.literal(name)];
   178	
   179	        let flags = 0;
   180	
   181	        if (binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') {
   182	                flags |= PROPS_IS_BINDABLE;
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        if (state.analysis.immutable) {
   186	                flags |= PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE;
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        if (state.analysis.runes) {
   190	                flags |= PROPS_IS_RUNES;
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        if (
   194	                state.analysis.accessors ||
   195	                (state.analysis.immutable
   196	                        ? binding.reassigned || (state.analysis.runes && binding.mutated)
   197	                        : binding.updated)
   198	        ) {
   199	                flags |= PROPS_IS_UPDATED;
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
   203	        let arg;
   204	
   205	        if (initial) {
   206	                // To avoid eagerly evaluating the right-hand-side, we wrap it in a thunk if necessary
   207	                if (is_simple_expression(initial)) {
   208	                        arg = initial;
   209	                } else {
   210	                        if (
   211	                                initial.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   212	                                initial.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
   213	                                initial.arguments.length === 0
   214	                        ) {
   215	                                arg = initial.callee;
   216	                        } else {
   217	                                arg = b.thunk(initial);
   218	                        }
   219	
   220	                        flags |= PROPS_IS_LAZY_INITIAL;
   221	                }
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        if (flags || arg) {
   225	                args.push(b.literal(flags));
   226	                if (arg) args.push(arg);
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        return b.call('$.prop', ...args);
   230	}
   231	
   232	/**
   233	 *
   234	 * @param {Binding} binding
   235	 * @param {ClientTransformState} state
   236	 * @returns
   237	 */
   238	export function is_prop_source(binding, state) {
   239	        return (
   240	                (binding.kind === 'prop' || binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') &&
   241	                (!state.analysis.runes ||
   242	                        state.analysis.accessors ||
   243	                        binding.reassigned ||
   244	                        binding.initial ||
   245	                        // Until legacy mode is gone, we also need to use the prop source when only mutated is true,
   246	                        // because the parent could be a legacy component which needs coarse-grained reactivity
   247	                        binding.updated)
   248	        );
   249	}
   250	
   251	/**
   252	 * @param {Expression} node
   253	 * @param {Scope | null} scope
   254	 */
   255	export function should_proxy(node, scope) {
   256	        if (
   257	                !node ||
   258	                node.type === 'Literal' ||
   259	                node.type === 'TemplateLiteral' ||
   260	                node.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' ||
   261	                node.type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
   262	                node.type === 'UnaryExpression' ||
   263	                node.type === 'BinaryExpression' ||
   264	                (node.type === 'Identifier' && node.name === 'undefined')
   265	        ) {
   266	                return false;
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        if (node.type === 'Identifier' && scope !== null) {
   270	                const binding = scope.get(node.name);
   271	                // Let's see if the reference is something that can be proxied
   272	                if (
   273	                        binding !== null &&
   274	                        !binding.reassigned &&
   275	                        binding.initial !== null &&
   276	                        binding.initial.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' &&
   277	                        binding.initial.type !== 'ClassDeclaration' &&
   278	                        binding.initial.type !== 'ImportDeclaration' &&
   279	                        binding.initial.type !== 'EachBlock' &&
   280	                        binding.initial.type !== 'SnippetBlock'
   281	                ) {
   282	                        return should_proxy(binding.initial, null);
   283	                }
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        return true;
   287	}
   288	
   289	/**
   290	 * Svelte legacy mode should use safe equals in most places, runes mode shouldn't
   291	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   292	 * @param {Expression} arg
   293	 */
   294	export function create_derived(state, arg) {
   295	        return b.call(state.analysis.runes ? '$.derived' : '$.derived_safe_equal', arg);
   296	}

2025-12-26 22:38:54,903 - INFO - swea-agent-sveltejs__svelte-16504 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me look more closely at the problem. The issue is about how the prop getter is created. Looking at props.js again:

When the `PROPS_IS_UPDATED` flag is 0 (line 357-359 in props.js), the function just returns a getter. This happens when the prop is never written to locally. However, the issue is that when this getter is used in a child component, the child component might not be tracking the right dependency.

Let me look at how props are accessed from $$props in the getter. The key part is:

```javascript
getter = () => {
    var value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
    if (value === undefined) return get_fallback();
    fallback_dirty = true;
    return value;
};
```

The getter accesses `props[key]`. Let me trace through what happens when a prop is passed to a child component. When we have:

```svelte
<!-- Parent -->
<script>
  let { onClick = () => {} } = $props();
</script>
<Child {onClick} />
```

The parent creates a prop getter that reads from `$$props.onClick`. When the parent passes this to the Child component, does it pass the value or a getter?

Looking at the component.js code (lines 168-197), when `has_state` is true, it wraps the value in a getter with `b.get(attribute.name, [b.return(value)])`. Otherwise it uses `b.init(attribute.name, value)`.

The issue is that when the parent reads `onClick` from its props and passes it to the child, if the parent has a default value, the prop system creates a derived or getter. But when passing it to the child, the question is whether the child receives the reactive getter or just the value.

Let me create a test to reproduce the issue:

import { test } from '"'"'../../test'"'"';

export default test({
	html: `
		<p>Count: 0</p>
		<p>Count2: 100</p>
		<button>Click</button>
		<button>Reset count to 50</button>
		<button>Reset count2 to 150</button>
	`,

	async test({ assert, target }) {
		const [clickBtn, resetBtn, reset2Btn] = target.querySelectorAll('"'"'button'"'"');

		// Click the button - should trigger handler and increment count
		flushSync(() => {
			clickBtn?.click();
		});

		assert.htmlEqual(
			target.innerHTML,
			`
				<p>Count: 1</p>
				<p>Count2: 100</p>
				<button>Click</button>
				<button>Reset count to 50</button>
				<button>Reset count2 to 150</button>
			`
		);

		// Reset count to 50
		flushSync(() => {
			resetBtn?.click();
		});

		assert.htmlEqual(
			target.innerHTML,
			`
				<p>Count: 50</p>
				<p>Count2: 100</p>
				<button>Click</button>
				<button>Reset count to 50</button>
				<button>Reset count2 to 150</button>
			`
		);

		// Click again - should increment from 50 to 51
		flushSync(() => {
			clickBtn?.click();
		});

		assert.htmlEqual(
			target.innerHTML,
			`
				<p>Count: 51</p>
				<p>Count2: 100</p>
				<button>Click</button>
				<button>Reset count to 50</button>
				<button>Reset count2 to 150</button>
			`
		);
	}
});

import * as fs from 'node:fs';
import * as path from 'node:path';
import { configDefaults, defineConfig } from 'vitest/config';

const pkg = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('packages/svelte/package.json', 'utf8'));

export default defineConfig({
	resolve: {
		alias: [
			{
				find: /^svelte\/?/,
				customResolver: (id, importer) => {
					// For some reason this turns up as "undefined" instead of "svelte/"
					const exported = pkg.exports[id === 'undefined' ? '.' : id.replace('undefined', './')];
					if (!exported) return;

					// When running the server version of the Svelte files,
					// we also want to use the server export of the Svelte package
					return path.resolve(
						'packages/svelte',
						importer?.includes('_output/server')
							? exported.default
							: exported.browser ?? exported.default
					);
				}
			}
		]
	},
	test: {
		dir: '.',

    34	                        rune === '$props'
    35	                ) {
    36	                        for (const path of paths) {
    37	                                // @ts-ignore this fails in CI for some insane reason
    38	                                const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(path.node.name));
    39	                                binding.kind =
    40	                                        rune === '$state'
    41	                                                ? 'state'
    42	                                                : rune === '$state.raw'
    43	                                                        ? 'raw_state'
    44	                                                        : rune === '$derived' || rune === '$derived.by'
    45	                                                                ? 'derived'
    46	                                                                : path.is_rest
    47	                                                                        ? 'rest_prop'
    48	                                                                        : 'prop';
    49	                        }
    50	                }
    51	
    52	                if (rune === '$props') {
    53	                        if (node.id.type !== 'ObjectPattern' && node.id.type !== 'Identifier') {
    54	                                e.props_invalid_identifier(node);
    55	                        }
    56	
    57	                        if (
    58	                                context.state.analysis.custom_element &&
    59	                                context.state.options.customElementOptions?.props == null
    60	                        ) {
    61	                                let warn_on;
    62	                                if (
    63	                                        node.id.type === 'Identifier' ||
    64	                                        (warn_on = node.id.properties.find((p) => p.type === 'RestElement')) != null
    65	                                ) {
    66	                                        w.custom_element_props_identifier(warn_on ?? node.id);
    67	                                }
    68	                        }
    69	
    70	                        context.state.analysis.needs_props = true;
    71	
    72	                        if (node.id.type === 'Identifier') {
    73	                                const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(node.id.name));
    74	                                binding.initial = null; // else would be $props()
    75	                                binding.kind = 'rest_prop';
    76	                        } else {
    77	                                equal(node.id.type, 'ObjectPattern');
    78	
    79	                                for (const property of node.id.properties) {
    80	                                        if (property.type !== 'Property') continue;
    81	
    82	                                        if (property.computed) {
    83	                                                e.props_invalid_pattern(property);
    84	                                        }
    85	
    86	                                        if (property.key.type === 'Identifier' && property.key.name.startsWith('$$')) {
    87	                                                e.props_illegal_name(property);
    88	                                        }
    89	
    90	                                        const value =
    91	                                                property.value.type === 'AssignmentPattern' ? property.value.left : property.value;
    92	
    93	                                        if (value.type !== 'Identifier') {
    94	                                                e.props_invalid_pattern(property);
    95	                                        }
    96	
    97	                                        const alias =
    98	                                                property.key.type === 'Identifier'
    99	                                                        ? property.key.name
   100	                                                        : String(/** @type {Literal} */ (property.key).value);
   101	
   102	                                        let initial = property.value.type === 'AssignmentPattern' ? property.value.right : null;
   103	
   104	                                        const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(value.name));
   105	                                        binding.prop_alias = alias;
   106	
   107	                                        // rewire initial from $props() to the actual initial value, stripping $bindable() if necessary
   108	                                        if (
   109	                                                initial?.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   110	                                                initial.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
   111	                                                initial.callee.name === '$bindable'
   112	                                        ) {
   113	                                                binding.initial = /** @type {Expression | null} */ (initial.arguments[0] ?? null);
   114	                                                binding.kind = 'bindable_prop';
   115	                                        } else {
   116	                                                binding.initial = initial;
   117	                                        }
   118	                                }
   119	                        }
   120	                }
   121	        } else {
   122	                if (node.init?.type === 'CallExpression') {
   123	                        const callee = node.init.callee;
   124	                        if (
   125	                                callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
   126	                                (callee.name === '$state' || callee.name === '$derived' || callee.name === '$props') &&
   127	                                context.state.scope.get(callee.name)?.kind !== 'store_sub'
   128	                        ) {
   129	                                e.rune_invalid_usage(node.init, callee.name);
   130	                        }
   131	                }
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        context.next();
   135	}
   136

   310	                                if (init != null && is_hoisted_function(init)) {
   311	                                        context.state.hoisted.push(
   312	                                                b.const(declarator.id, /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(init)))
   313	                                        );
   314	
   315	                                        continue;
   316	                                }
   317	
   318	                                declarations.push(/** @type {VariableDeclarator} */ (context.visit(declarator)));
   319	                                continue;
   320	                        }
   321	
   322	                        if (has_props) {
   323	                                if (declarator.id.type !== 'Identifier') {
   324	                                        // Turn export let into props. It's really really weird because export let { x: foo, z: [bar]} = ..
   325	                                        // means that foo and bar are the props (i.e. the leafs are the prop names), not x and z.
   326	                                        const tmp = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('tmp'));
   327	                                        const { inserts, paths } = extract_paths(declarator.id, tmp);
   328	
   329	                                        declarations.push(
   330	                                                b.declarator(
   331	                                                        tmp,
   332	                                                        /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(/** @type {Expression} */ (declarator.init)))
   333	                                                )
   334	                                        );
   335	
   336	                                        for (const { id, value } of inserts) {
   337	                                                id.name = context.state.scope.generate('$$array');
   338	                                                context.state.transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };
   339	
   340	                                                const expression = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(b.thunk(value)));
   341	                                                declarations.push(b.declarator(id, b.call('$.derived', expression)));
   342	                                        }
   343	
   344	                                        for (const path of paths) {
   345	                                                const name = /** @type {Identifier} */ (path.node).name;
   346	                                                const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(name));
   347	                                                const value = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(path.expression));
   348	
   349	                                                declarations.push(
   350	                                                        b.declarator(
   351	                                                                path.node,
   352	                                                                binding.kind === 'bindable_prop'
   353	                                                                        ? get_prop_source(binding, context.state, binding.prop_alias ?? name, value)
   354	                                                                        : value
   355	                                                        )
   356	                                                );
   357	                                        }
   358	
   359	                                        continue;
   360	                                }
   361	
   362	                                const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(declarator.id.name));
   363	
   364	                                declarations.push(
   365	                                        b.declarator(
   366	                                                declarator.id,
   367	                                                get_prop_source(
   368	                                                        binding,
   369	                                                        context.state,
   370	                                                        binding.prop_alias ?? declarator.id.name,
   371	                                                        declarator.init && /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(declarator.init))
   372	                                                )
   373	                                        )
   374	                                );
   375	
   376	                                continue;
   377	                        }
   378	
   379	                        declarations.push(
   380	                                ...create_state_declarators(
   381	                                        declarator,
   382	                                        context,
   383	                                        /** @type {Expression} */ (declarator.init && context.visit(declarator.init))
   384	                                )
   385	                        );
   386	                }
   387	        }
   388	
   389	        if (declarations.length === 0) {
   390	                return b.empty;
   391	        }
   392	
   393	        return {
   394	                ...node,
   395	                declarations
   396	        };
   397	}
   398	
   399	/**
   400	 * Creates the output for a state declaration in legacy mode.
   401	 * @param {VariableDeclarator} declarator
   402	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   403	 * @param {Expression} value
   404	 */
   405	function create_state_declarators(declarator, context, value) {
   406	        if (declarator.id.type === 'Identifier') {
   407	                return [
   408	                        b.declarator(
   409	                                declarator.id,
   410	                                b.call('$.mutable_source', value, context.state.analysis.immutable ? b.true : undefined)
   411	                        )
   412	                ];
   413	        }
   414	
   415	        const tmp = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('tmp'));
   416	        const { inserts, paths } = extract_paths(declarator.id, tmp);
   417	
   418	        return [
   419	                b.declarator(tmp, value),
   420	                ...inserts.map(({ id, value }) => {
   421	                        id.name = context.state.scope.generate('$$array');
   422	                        context.state.transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };
   423	
   424	                        const expression = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(b.thunk(value)));
   425	                        return b.declarator(id, b.call('$.derived', expression));
   426	                }),
   427	                ...paths.map((path) => {
   428	                        const value = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(path.expression));
   429	                        const binding = context.state.scope.get(/** @type {Identifier} */ (path.node).name);
   430	
   431	                        return b.declarator(
   432	                                path.node,
   433	                                binding?.kind === 'state'
   434	                                        ? b.call('$.mutable_source', value, context.state.analysis.immutable ? b.true : undefined)
   435	                                        : value
   436	                        );
   437	                })
   438	        ];
   439	}
   440

    13	 * @param {Array<AST.Attribute | AST.SpreadAttribute>} attributes

    15	 * @param {AST.StyleDirective[]} style_directives
